20/12/2023, 11:17 - Charan  Rkv: //n quuen 
#include<stdio.h>
#include<math.h>
int n;
int c=0;
int x[100];
int place(int k,int i){
	for(int j=1;j<=k-1;j++){
		if(x[j]==i ||( (j-x[j])==(k-i)) || ((j+x[j])==(k+i))){
			return 0;
		}
	}
	return 1;
}
void print_sol(int n){
	c++;
	for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
		for(int j=1;j<=n;j++){
			if(x[i]==j){ 
				printf("q%d is (%d %d)",i,i,x[i]);
			}
		}
	}
}		
void nqueen(int k,int n){
	for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
		if(place(k,i)==1){
			x[k]=i;
			printf("k=%d i=%d\n",k,i);
			if(k==n){
				print_sol(n);
			}
			else{
				nqueen(k+1,n);
			}
		}
	}
}
int main(){
	printf("enter the no of queens=");
	scanf("%d",&n);
	nqueen(1,n);
	printf("total no .of solutions=%d",c);
}

datasource db {
  provider = "mysql" // or "postgresql" if using PostgreSQL
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

model User {
  id             Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  name           String
  currentJob     Job?     @relation("CurrentJob", fields: [currentJobId], references: [id])
  currentJobId   Int?
  applyingJobs   Job[]    @relation("ApplyingJobs")
}

model Job {
  id       Int    @id @default(autoincrement())
  title    String
  user     User?  @relation("CurrentJob")
  applicants User[] @relation("ApplyingJobs")
  post     Post?  @relation(fields: [postId], references: [id])
  postId   Int?
}

model Post {
  id   Int    @id @default(autoincrement())
  title String
  job   Job   @relation
}
29/10/2024, 19:05 - Balaji: generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "mysql" // Change to "postgresql" if using PostgreSQL
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

model User {
  id             Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  name           String
  currentJobId   Int?     // Foreign key to current Job
  currentJob     Job?     @relation("CurrentJob", fields: [currentJobId], references: [id])
  applyingJobs   Job[]    @relation("ApplyingJobs")
}

model Job {
  id         Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  title      String
  userId     Int?     // Foreign key to User
  user       User?    @relation("CurrentJob", fields: [userId], references: [id])
  applicants  User[]   @relation("ApplyingJobs")
  postId     Int?     // Foreign key to Post
  post       Post?     @relation(fields: [postId], references: [id])
}

model Post {
  id    Int    @id @default(autoincrement())
  title String
  job   Job?   @relation
}
